THIRD-PARTY SOFTWARE NOTICES
==============================================================================

ShrimpDocViewer's WebAssembly core is compiled from Rust and statically includes the
third-party crates listed below. Each is distributed under a permissive license
(MIT / Apache-2.0 / BSD-2-Clause / BSD-3-Clause / Zlib / Unicode-3.0 / 0BSD /
Unlicense). Their copyright notices and license texts are reproduced here, as the
licenses require, even though ShrimpDocViewer ships only the compiled binary.

The bundled font (fonts/NotoSansTC-VF.ttf, Noto Sans TC) is covered separately by
fonts/OFL.txt (SIL Open Font License 1.1). The runtime npm dependency
@embedpdf/pdfium carries its own LICENSE files within its package.
